Important News

National Army Captures Yanxia, Defeats Remnants of Bandits in Eastern Hubei, Recovers Lijiaji 92

A correspondent from Hankou reports that after capturing Longgang on the 3rd of this month, the bandit suppression troops in southern Hubei, led by Guo Rudong and Zhang Gang, immediately pursued the bandit lair at Yanxia in victory. The area is surrounded by mountains on all sides, making it even more dangerous than Longgang. The bandits, led by Kong, have been entrenched here for several years. The bandits' arrangements originally placed equal importance on the area and Longgang, with each acting as a horn to the other. Important organizations were divided between the two places. Sanxikou and other locations served as the gateway. To the right of Yanxia was Jin Kangyuan, where the pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Provincial Arsenal was located. On the 3rd of this month, after Guo and Zhang's troops occupied Longgang, they immediately redistributed their forces, with Guo's troops attacking Yanxia and Zhang's troops attacking Jin Kangyuan. Guo's 76th Brigade, led by Ji Hanxun, including the 151st Regiment, 154th Regiment, and the Brigade Headquarters' pistol squad, led by Huang, set out at dawn on the 4th, advancing along Huangqiao, Xinpu, Dawangmiao, and Tangshan, searching as they went. About two thousand bandits, relying on the line of the Lion Rock, Ke Mountain, and 家之 (transliteration), made contact with government troops. In the midst of the battle, over a hundred red flags were discovered near Chengxian, on the right flank of the position, with wild cries resounding throughout the mountains. Brigade Commander Huang immediately ordered Tang 霖 (transliteration), commander of the 151st Regiment, to lead six companies to attack the bandits on the right flank. By 8:00 AM, the bandits began to falter. Seeing Tang's regiment approaching, they fled towards Sheweishan and Liyan. Pursuing troops followed closely, and after passing through Caijialong and Zhongjialong, they fled in disarray towards the Tongbeitoushan area. The brigade completely occupied the bandit lair at Yanxia at 2:00 PM. In this battle, over four hundred Red bandits were killed, over eight hundred were wounded, over forty were captured alive, and a large amount of spoils of war and reactionary documents were seized. Government troops also suffered casualties, with six company commanders killed, over ten wounded, over sixty soldiers killed, and over seventy wounded. When Guo's division attacked Yanxia, Zhang's division sent troops to attack the bandits' right flank via Shiyan, and also sent Zhu's regiment to launch a fierce attack on Jin Kangyuan, while coordinating with Huang's brigade. When Zhu's regiment approached Jin Kangyuan, about three or four hundred bandits guarding the arsenal opened fire fiercely on the regiment. After the regiment divided its forces and launched a brave attack, the bandits suffered heavy losses and fled in different directions towards Dadun and the deep mountains and forests. The unit also recovered Jin Kangyuan. An inspection of the arsenal revealed the words "Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Provincial Arsenal" written in large characters at the entrance. The structure was magnificent and large in scale. In addition to transporting the gun-making machinery back, the various gun, artillery, ammunition, and bomb manufacturing machines were too bulky to transport and were all destroyed, and the factory site was burned to the ground. The remnants of the bandits, having lost their stronghold, fled to the border of Hunan and Jiangxi overnight, hoping to join forces with another group of Kong's bandits. They are currently being pursued and intercepted separately by troops from the three provinces and will soon be completely eliminated. He Chengjun originally planned to depart on the 5th to oversee the suppression, but upon hearing of the recovery of Yanxia, he has cancelled his trip. As for the eastern Hubei area, the situation had previously been tense but has now become peaceful. The bandits who had entrenched themselves in Jinjiazai have disintegrated and fled in two groups. The majority was led by Xu Xiangqian, and a smaller group was led by Cai Shenxi, fleeing towards Huangma and Taihu. Xu is the most fierce bandit leader in the pseudo-Fourth Front Army, and Cai is the successor to Kuang Jixun after his assassination. Combining the remnants of various pseudo-divisions, totaling about tens of thousands, the main force invaded 圑陂 (Tuan Pi) on the 2nd and captured Lijiaji in Huanggang County. Hao Luoling, commander of the 54th Division, received the report and urgently ordered the cavalry company stationed in 圑陂 (Tuan Pi) to hold their ground and wait for reinforcements. He then personally led the entire division, traveling hundreds of miles at night via Xiaojia’ao and Luotian, to intercept the bandits. Upon arriving near 圑陂 (Tuan Pi) on the 3rd, he learned that cavalry company commander Chen Zhong, with a single company, had defended against tens of thousands of bandits. Although the sacrifices were great, 圑陂 (Tuan Pi) was preserved. He then ordered the Guo and Liu brigades to take the lead in the attack, and after fierce hand-to-hand combat, they finally defeated the bandits, killing about several thousand, and seizing countless spoils. Hao, knowing that the bandits had fled northwest, again led his troops in pursuit. On the 5th, they passed through the Xinzhou area, and on the 6th, they recovered Lijiaji, capturing over three thousand prisoners. Many more were killed on the spot. The group of Cai's bandits who fled to Taihu, numbering about seven or eight thousand, fled eastward from Jinjiapu. Division Commander Shangguan Yunxiang immediately led his troops in pursuit, engaging in fierce battles for an entire day in Daxiaowenchong and Hetoup. The bandits dispersed, and it is estimated that over two thousand five hundred bandits were captured, along with over a hundred horses and over three hundred rifles. In addition, the He bandits in central Hubei have suffered repeated losses in the Jing and Zhong counties. Xiao of Chu telegraphed that the remnants are currently in the vicinity of the Dahong Mountain and west of Liu Fangzui. The National Army completed its encirclement on the 5th and will soon annihilate them. It is also rumored that He himself originally fled to Jun County when he fled to Nanzhang, attempting to enter Shaanxi. The bandits in Jing and Zhong may be another group of He's bandits (October 6th).

Chiang Kai-shek Returns to Hankou from Lushan 93

Issues Orders and Sample Rural Land Handling Regulations, Orders Hubei, Anhui, and Henan Provinces to Implement Seriously

A correspondent from Hankou reports that after a brief rest in Lushan, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has returned to Hankou to oversee the thorough suppression of the Red bandits, the restoration of rural areas, and the stabilization of order. He descended the mountain from Guling on the 5th to Xunyang, and in the evening, he boarded the Yongji warship to travel west. He arrived in Hankou at 9:00 AM on the 6th. His entourage, as well as Mr. Wang Shuhan and Bao Wenbo, also arrived on commercial ships. After landing, Chiang went to the Yihe Village residence to meet with He Chengjun, the director of the Suppression Commission, and inquired about the recent bandit suppression situation. He then met with Liu Quji, the administrative supervisor of the Eighth District, and the newly appointed Mayor of Hankou, Wu Guozhen, as well as the Director of Public Security, Chen Xizeng. It was decided that on the 7th, he would meet with Xu Yuanquan, commander of the Tenth Army, Xia Douyin, chairman of the provincial government, and Li Jue, commander of the 19th Division. Chiang believes that with the Red bandits about to be suppressed, refugees urgently need to be resettled. He also emphasized that the restoration of rural areas should be given special attention. He has specially formulated regulations for handling rural land in the bandit-suppressed areas of various provinces, which have been promulgated and implemented. On the 6th, he issued instructions to the governments of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces to be informed and to act accordingly. The original order is as follows:

"Land is the source of food for the people and the mother of wealth. The importance of production tools is recorded in historical records. Throughout Chinese history, dynastic changes and great turmoil have invariably originated from the decline of rural areas and the desolation of fields. Since the Red bandits have run rampant, they have used the destruction of rural areas as a means of eliminating the nation, nominally dividing land but actually neglecting cultivation. This has led to frequent famines and widespread poverty. The situation is particularly dire in the provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi. Now that the officers and soldiers have bravely suppressed the bandits, refugees everywhere are urgently awaiting resettlement. This Commander-in-Chief feels deeply concerned and cannot bear to perpetuate the remnants of the land division, making innocent people suffer the sacrifices of the Red scourge. Nor is it desired to gain the sympathy of rich farmers, giving assets special protection. People of all levels in rural areas, regardless of wealth, intelligence, or ignorance, should be brought into order, so that there is an adjustment of surpluses and deficiencies, and no conflicts of interest. Based on this principle, the regulations for handling rural land in the bandit-suppressed areas of various provinces are formulated, promulgated, and implemented. To revitalize agriculture and promote agricultural development, the establishment of cooperatives is fundamentally important. However, in the aftermath of great chaos, there is a division between the flourishing and the withered, and different aspirations. Simple organization is needed to meet urgent needs, and subtle insight is needed to achieve impartial investigation. Before rural cooperatives are established, a rural revitalization committee should be established as an organization for transitional handling. Hence, there is the first chapter of regulations. Article 7 of China's Land Law recognizes private land ownership. The Premier advocated for a slight land value tax, also taking recognition of private land ownership as a prerequisite. Therefore, for land that has been dispersed by bandits, if there are deeds and boundaries, the deeds will be submitted for review. If there are no deeds but there are boundaries, certificates will be submitted for review. Once completed, the land will be returned to the original owner, which is not only in line with national conditions but also deeply in accordance with the principles of the Party. Hence, there is the second chapter of regulations. If boundaries have been destroyed, the land has lost its original form, and deeds are lost and difficult to find, this kind of dispute cannot be resolved by the methods of the previous chapter. Therefore, adopting the spirit of land consolidation laws of various countries, a meeting of landowners is convened for public review, and the intention of exchanging cultivated land is implied in the resolution of disputes. Hence, there is the third chapter of regulations. All land whose ownership has not been determined or that is ownerless will be managed and allocated by the Rural Revitalization Committee for cultivation. However, owner-farmers and landlords, as well as various types of agricultural laborers, should each be granted a certain amount of land based on population. What procedures should be followed? After landowners recover their managed properties, can they change or restore tenant farmers? There should be clear standards set. Hence, there is the fourth chapter of regulations. Resettling refugees starts with protecting tenant farmers and hired laborers. The legislative examples of various modern countries all regard reducing land rents, securing tenancy rights, and implementing a compensation system as the three key factors in protecting tenant farmers. If any of these three factors is missing, the goal of protection cannot be achieved. Hence, there is the fifth chapter of regulations. The theory of limiting land ownership originated with Dong Zhongshu in the Western Han dynasty and was further developed by Jia Sidao in the Southern Song dynasty. The method was relatively complete. China's Land Law also has provisions for limiting the maximum amount of land ownership. Today, collecting income tax according to Guohuai's method, compared to the system of land fees being nationalized and redistributed in various countries, although there is a distinction between gradual and rapid progress, they are both social policies. To increase the wealth of the many by benefiting the few, it is necessary to adapt to local conditions. Hence, there is the sixth chapter of regulations. Relieving farmers' debts must be supported by promoting rural cooperatives and farmers' banks, with credit cooperatives being particularly necessary. At a time when finances are depleted, raising funds is extremely difficult. Now, the agricultural products, land rents, wages, and rents from public land, managed by the Rural Revitalization Committee, as well as the income tax collected under the progressive system, are stored and loaned to various cooperatives to be used for financing agriculture. That is, what is taken from the rural areas is still returned to the rural public. Hence, there is the seventh chapter of regulations. Although the Rural Revitalization Committee is a temporary organization, it has great responsibilities and heavy burdens. On the one hand, designated funding should be provided; on the other hand, malpractice should be prevented, so as to avoid long-term neglect and hinder the formation of rural cooperatives. Hence, there is the eighth chapter of regulations. If the above-mentioned measures are only implemented in the bandit-affected counties, the scope would be too narrow and the results would be difficult to achieve. For a more comprehensive approach, in order to ensure the soundness of the rural economy and prevent the incitement of the Red bandits, rural committees should also be organized and promoted separately in counties that have not been affected by banditry, but the term "revitalization" should not be used to show the distinction. Hence, there are the provisions in Article 6, Article 47, Article 51, and Article 59. In summary, the second and third chapters are designed to protect landlords and owner-farmers, the fifth and seventh chapters are designed to protect tenant farmers and hired laborers, the fourth and sixth chapters are the linchpin for harmonizing the interests of all levels, and the first and eighth chapters are the mechanisms and effects for advancing the linchpin. If the provisions of these regulations are fully implemented, the land in each rural area will gradually be managed by rural cooperatives, and all members of the cooperatives will be users of the land, without the distinction between landlords, owner-farmers, tenant farmers, and hired laborers. Then, the Premier's proposition of 'those who till the land shall own it' will not be difficult to gradually realize, and the methods of thoroughly improving agriculture will also be effectively implemented. This Commander-in-Chief has high hopes and hereby orders the provincial government to take note and comply, and to instruct its subordinates to comply as well (October 6th)."

The Miserable Situation in Laizhou, Under Siege 94

A correspondent from Jinan reports that Laizhou is currently surrounded on three sides by provincial troops. Liu's army is desperately defending the city, and they have been in a stalemate for many days. The suffering of the people in the city from the ravages of war is beyond description. Mr. 某 (transliteration), the stationmaster of the Laizhou station on the Jiaolai highway, escaped with his wife and children on the 29th of last month. According to him, the situation inside the city is beyond recovery. In order to win over his subordinates, Liu Zhennian ordered soldiers to go out of the city in shifts to confront the enemy. Those who remain in the city act as they please. Currently, the doors and windows of the people have been dismantled by the troops for building fortifications. Every household is left open, allowing soldiers to enter and exit freely, take property at will, and rape women at will. This coming and going is almost like a revolving lantern. As a result, countless women have drowned themselves in wells or hanged themselves. From 南門里 (South Gate) to the intersection, the houses have been burned and bombed completely. He was fortunate to be acquainted with a regimental attachment and begged in every possible way before being allowed to escape. Each person was only allowed to wear a single layer of clothing; all other items were forbidden to be taken out. If the war continues to be prolonged, it is feared that there will be no survivors left among the people of Laizhou.

According to a Mr. 某 (transliteration) in the education field who escaped, Liu Zhennian has recently been very active in training his troops and preparing military supplies and food. For several days before the outbreak of the war, he frequently mobilized troops. At first, people did not pay much attention, but on September 18th, the city was filled with armed soldiers patrolling back and forth, paying close attention to pedestrians. They also frequently went to various agencies and schools, asking about "people sent by the provincial government," and inquired especially diligently about the business tax bureau, asking "Is the director in?" as many as five or six times. Those in the know began to suspect that something was about to happen. Since the outbreak of the war, the entire city has been in a war zone. Schools have been closed and used to billet troops. Various agencies have also been in great disarray, and those who were relocating clogged the roads. Soldiers actively engaged in defensive works, digging trenches, and forcibly removing doors and windows from residents' homes. Merchants' food supplies were completely sealed off and not allowed to be moved without permission. In addition, 40,000 bags of flour were transported into the city from behind the Hai Temple as a plan for prolonged defense. The entire city was under a state of emergency martial law, and all affairs were handled by military orders. The extent of the people's fear can be imagined. Civilian goods were requisitioned, and demands were frequent and urgent. Dong Yushan, the president of the Chamber of Commerce, was forced to jump into a well and died. Currently, the city of Laizhou is packed with troops, numbering no less than ten thousand, completely a military world. Most of the personnel of various agencies have already fled. The director of the postal bureau has also fled to the northern countryside. In the past, mail to Yantai mostly passed through Laizhou by highway, but now it is detoured through Pingdu to Yantai. Recently, the shelling has been intense, and the tall buildings on all four gates have been completely destroyed by fire. Eight or nine out of ten houses in the city have also been demolished, leaving behind a scene of rubble. The essence of the entire city has been almost completely destroyed (October 6th).

Continues Research on Various Industrial Projects by the Inspection Groups

The work of the Shaanxi Industrial Inspection Groups' north and south groups in Shaanxi has ended, and they have returned to Zhengzhou one after another to sort out their reports. Hunan National Martial Arts Examination Situation 96

Almost Resulted in a Duel Between the Northern and Southern Factions, the Top Three Were All Students of the Northern Faction

A correspondent from Changsha reports that the second Hunan National Martial Arts Examination established a National Examination Committee two months ago, inviting national martial arts masters and Party, government, and military leaders from both inside and outside the province to serve as committee members. A notice was sent to all counties and cities to send three to five candidates to the province by the end of September. The examination was scheduled to begin on October 1st. A total of 280 instructors and students were sent from various counties and cities, national martial arts training institutes, and technical training brigades. Among them, about fifty or sixty were sent by training institutes and technical teams, and the rest were sent by various counties and cities. The technical team hired Li Lijiug, a famous Taijiquan master from Hebei, as the team leader to teach national martial arts to military officers and soldiers. The training institute hired Wan Laisheng, a famous teacher from the north, as the director. Wan has now left his position and is managed by Gu Ruzhang, who specializes in teaching national martial arts to the general public. Regardless of gender or age, anyone can enroll. Li, Gu, and others teach the Northern Wudang style of long fist, which is very easy to attack with. Most of the national martial artists in Hunan practice the Southern Wu style of short fist, which emphasizes defense. Liu Senyan, a well-known warrior in Hunan Province, wrote to Gu Ruzhang several months ago to arrange a match, but Chairman He stopped it. Half a month before this examination, Gu again wrote to Liu to ask them to compete alone on the first day of the examination. Liu agreed, and the letter contained words such as "I will go even if there are ten thousand people." As a result, the citizens of Changsha were eagerly awaiting the duel between Gu and Liu, which had been brewing for several months, hoping that the victory and defeat of the northern and southern factions could be determined. Unexpectedly, He Jian denied the request, and Liu Senyan was still required to participate in the preliminary examination according to the rules. Liu complied with the order because he still had the opportunity to compete with Gu at the final duel. However, the results of the first two days of the examination showed that the Northern long fist had a significant advantage because it specialized in hitting the opponent's head and eyes and was lively and agile. The Southern short fist, which specialized in defense, was often beaten until its head was bruised and its eyes were swollen. On the second day, when Liu Senyan competed with Ning Desheng, a technical team student who practiced northern fist, Liu initially had the upper hand. Later, due to Liu's carelessness, he was grabbed by Ning, and the two hugged each other and fell to the ground at the same time. Liu was about to rise when the examiner Xin Jianhou (who had won first place in national martial arts in Fengtian) suddenly took advantage of the opportunity to separate the two and punched Liu twice, which angered the audience. They believed that the northerners were helping each other and attacking the southerners. The whole venue was in an uproar, causing a major dispute. Because Xin's attack on Liu was confirmed, He Jian publicly stripped Xin of his uniform, arrested him, and punished him. The storm subsided. However, as a result, Southern masters such as Tang Huidian (who won first place in the national examination last year) were willing to forfeit and refused to appear. A great rift developed between the Northern and Southern factions. On the evening of that day, dozens of people suddenly surrounded Liu's residence, and their intentions were unknown. Liu quietly fled. When the Garrison Command and the Public Security Bureau sent military police to protect him, the crowd had already dispersed. Only one suspect, Liu Fengxiang, was arrested and sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. As a result, Liu felt quite threatened. At 4:00 PM the following afternoon, Gu Ruzhang was passing through Fuzheng Street in a car when someone suddenly took his hat and threw it on the ground. The Northern and Southern factions became even more hostile. He Jian heard the report and believed that the original intention of allowing guest instructors to participate in the examination was to unite the various factions from the north and south into one, but it had actually developed into a major duel between the Northern and Southern factions, which was a great loss to the promotion of national martial arts. Therefore, it was decided that starting from the third day, all guest instructors would not be allowed to participate in the examination. Only national martial artists from Hunan were allowed to participate. However, although the instructors of the training institute and the technical brigade were northerners, the students were all from Hunan, so they were still allowed to participate in the test in order to eliminate all disputes. As a result, Liu and Gu had no chance to compete. On the third day of the examination, Liu still appeared and won. The examination period was originally set for three days, but because it could not be completed, it was extended by one day. On the fourth day, the final was held. Liu also appeared twice, first knocking down Wu Shihai and then Wang Shaoyun. This examination had a quota of thirty people, and Liu was recorded within the thirty people. When the final thirty-person final was held, Liu suddenly disappeared. He could not be found everywhere. Until the final four-person final, Liu arrived at the meeting again by car. He Jian felt that he was not following the rules and was very displeased. The audience applauded and welcomed Liu to participate in the examination again; otherwise, they would refund the tickets (because the audience bought tickets to enter the venue, with ticket prices divided into two grades of 50 cents and one yuan). But the opportunity had passed and there was no way to remedy the situation. Liu reported at the entrance of the stage that in order to protect his life, he voluntarily gave up the competition and asked the public to forgive him. At this time, some people advocated arresting him, so Liu immediately left the stage and rushed away after reporting. At this point, the final four-person final was completed and the examination was over. The first four were: first place, Liu Xinquan; second place, Liu Shu; third place, Liu Huizhan; and fourth place, Liu Zaixing. The order of the fifth place and below was determined separately by the committee. It is heard that among the thirty people selected, except for Liu Senyan, who practiced Southern boxing, most were students from national martial arts training institutes and technical brigades. Therefore, this Hunan national martial arts examination saw a complete victory for the Northern boxing (October 5th).

Two Major Libraries in the Jiangsu Provincial Capital 97

"May Third" and "Zhenjiang" are Both Actively Preparing

There are recently two relatively large libraries in the Jiangsu provincial capital that have roughly taken shape and are currently being actively prepared. Their general situations are described below:

The May Third Library is located outside the Ximen of Zhenjiang. The multi-story building began construction in August of last year. However, due to the outbreak of the Shanghai Incident, construction was suspended for a long time. Only recently was it completed. The library's expenses totaled more than 20,000 yuan, all from fines from the former Anti-Japanese Association and donated funds raised. About 5,000 types of books have been collected. It is heard that the library will first open the reading room and the research room for issues related to Japan in the near future, and the rest of the departments will be opened gradually. The official opening date will be after all the construction is completed.

Zhenjiang Library: After renting the former site of the provincial Party headquarters at Taiping Bridge as the site of the Provincial Zhenjiang Library, the library began renovating the premises, ordering custom furniture, and purchasing books. The renovation project will be completed within a few days. Tables, chairs, bookshelves, and other furniture are also being rushed to completion. For thoroughness, the library sent personnel to visit major libraries in Beijing and Shanghai and discussed the advantages and disadvantages of various equipment plans with experts to choose the best options. For the purchase of books, it is planned to start with social sciences and natural sciences. For old Chinese books, it is planned to obtain them through donations, storage, and exchanges. Currently, more than 3,700 books have been donated from various parties, more than 3,300 have been stored, and more than 180 periodical publications have been ordered. It is estimated that by the end of the first year, the number of Chinese and Western books donated and ordered will reach at least more than 15,000. The education department has approved an appropriation of 40,000 yuan for this year. The library plans to use 30,000 yuan to purchase books and equipment and 10,000 yuan for salaries and operating expenses. If it can be expanded according to plan year by year, it will undoubtedly become a grand spectacle of provincial documentation. The library originally planned to open the newspaper and magazine rooms around the Double Tenth Festival, but in order to enrich the content, it is heard that they will all be opened when the library is officially established.

Songjiang 98

Accusation Against the Police Chief at Court: Shen Jingxi, the former police chief of this county, had pursued Minister Niu Yongjian for many years. Because of this, he had a deep friendship with Yin Shisheng, a local gentry and fellow student. Recently, due to the robbery case of the Xingye Bank, which was presided over by Mr. Hui, Mr. Yin appealed to the province to issue a letter of instruction, which caused some misunderstanding. Furthermore, the branch chief Shi Wenhuan requested leave of absence, owing more than 400 yuan in unpaid rent. Despite repeated demands, the money had not been paid. Chief Shen presented a petition to the county government, urging a strict investigation and demanding that Shi pay the money. Branch Chief Shi is the younger brother of Madam Yin Shi Yaxiong. Madam Yin claimed that Chief Shen owed Yin 200 yuan from his time in Kunshan, which with interest amounted to 408 yuan. The previous evening, she went to the Public Security Bureau to settle the account. Shen did not acknowledge the interest, leading to a dispute. It almost escalated into a violent clash. Zhu Shikui, an inspector at the bureau, advised Madam Yin to leave. For some unknown reason, she fell to the ground and fainted. Yin Shisheng happened to be in Songjiang due to the Songhu Automobile Company's trial run in Songjiang. Upon hearing of this incident, he telegraphed the county magistrate and the president of the court to come to the bureau to mediate. The day before yesterday, Madam Shi, with apparent bruising and purple marks on her arm, filed a complaint with the court. Because the procedure was not in accordance, it was transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation. This morning (the 7th) at 10 o'clock, the investigative court was opened. The plaintiff was Yin Shi Yaxiong, the defendant was Shen Jing (represented by Gu Shuxuan). Witnesses County Government Secretary Tang Zhan Sheng, Public Security Bureau Section Chief Yu Shifang, and Accounting Bureau Official Yi Yao, all complied with the summons to appear in court. Madam Yin has also alleged that she was humiliated while demanding repayment of debt and that the chief used his power to commit violence, and has telegraphed the provincial offices requesting his removal. Both sides are simultaneously pursuing administrative and judicial avenues. It is expected that their dispute will not be easily resolved in the short term.

In Yangjia Village, Zhouzhuang, in the county, a bandit boat arrived on the 26th of last month, carrying eight or nine bandits armed with weapons. They broke into the home of villager Tang Ali and robbed him. Before leaving, they kidnapped Tang's wife, Madam Shen, and his nine-year-old second son, Xiao Di. Changshu

Xu Zhao's Remains Transported to Zhenru for Re-examination 102

The case of the unexplained death of Tianzhuang farmer Xu Zhao has been reported by local citizens Yang Zhenmin and Yang Qiyu. As a result, the county government requested the High Court to send a forensic examiner Xuan Fang to Changshu for examination. The bone steaming autopsy was performed on September 17th and 18th. According to the judgment of forensic examiner Xuan, there were no new injuries, and it was determined that she had fallen into the river and died before death. Thereupon the county government immediately detained the original informants Yang Qiyu and others. However, afterwards there were many rumors, saying that this bone steaming autopsy was based on the "Washing Away of Wrongs", and there were many discrepancies. There was also much dissatisfaction with Xuan Fang's judgment. At that time, the entire city was in an uproar, but Yang and others are still detained and have not yet been sentenced. In order to suppress the dissatisfaction outside, Examiner Huang Cheng especially brought Yang and others to court for questioning on the afternoon of the 5th, and informed them that there were many criticisms of this case, and that the entire case file would be transferred to the High Court for review. The remains will be transported to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for re-examination, in order to show great fairness. Yang and others agreed, but requested permission to be released on bail. Examiner Huang Cheng was unable to approve the request before the case was resolved.

Wuxi

Flour Merchants Request Withdrawal of Patrol Boats 103

Since the Ministry of Finance implemented the unified tax in the Republic of China's 17th year (1928), the measures have been changed three times in four years. After the implementation of the new regulations by the unified tax management office last month, patrol boats were re-established at various key points on the river routes, and inspectors were assigned to check passing ships. If there were no sub-transportation documents for cloth, cotton yarn, flour, etc., regardless of retail or wholesale, they were immediately detained. In a few days, Dingsheng, Hengxie, and Taifeng flour mills, as well as Demao Sen cloth store, etc., were fined because they were shipping goods from the flour and yarn factories in this county without sub-transportation documents. These companies have successively sent letters to the Chamber of Commerce, forwarding them to the unified tax office, requesting the repeal of the new regulations. The flour mills in the interior have also stated that the unified tax management office's establishment of patrol boats on the river routes is far more harmful than the previous transit duty stations. Due to the inconvenience of transshipment, the operations of the various mills have been hindered. Maoxin and Jiufeng, among others, have already stopped production. The Flour Mill Association of the interior of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, as well as the Shanghai Flour Mill Association, jointly petitioned the Ministry of Finance and the unified tax office to change the new regulations and immediately withdraw the patrol boats, which are essentially a disguised transit duty station, in order to facilitate the transportation of goods and avoid difficulties in the south.

Night Boat from Wuxi to Yuyao Robbed 104

Recently, water robbery cases have emerged one after another. According to yesterday's (7th) news, the night boat from Wuxi to Yuyao was robbed again in Wuxi. The boat was moored under the Tonghui bridge in Wuxi. The boat owner's name is Zhou Shifu. There are four shifts leaving at 7 p.m. every day. The previous (6th) day, as usual, the boat left Wuxi for Yuyao. When passing through the Baimu village area, Huangcaodu, approximately 10 p.m., it was suddenly encountered by a pirate boat. More than a dozen pirates jumped out, one pirate held a pistol, and the other pirates held knives and clubs. Speaking in a Northern accent, wearing short clothes and blue cloth on their heads, they ordered the boat to stop. When the boat owner Zhou Shifu saw the situation, he had to stop the boat. The pirates went from boat to boat and beat the crew members arbitrarily. Then, they arbitrarily searched and robbed, totaling a loss of more than 400 yuan. After the pirates obtained their loot, they sped away to the north. Yesterday morning at 11 a.m., boat owner Zhou Shifu reported the robbery to the shipping association, which in turn reported it to the county government. At 1 p.m., Section Chief Wang opened a court to question him, and ordered him to return home and wait for the police to be dispatched to investigate and arrest the pirates and bring them to justice.

Kidnapping Case from Shazhou Solved in Beijing 105

Shao Tang, the eleven-year-old son of Dr. Li Zhongtang, from Deji Street, Liuyu Dai, Shazhou Third District, was kidnapped by bandits on July 27th of this year. Zhenjiang

Provincial Jurong Road to Open on the 12th 106

In order to facilitate transportation between the provincial capital and Jurong, the Jiangsu Construction Department trialed a long-distance bus service on the provincial Jurong road this spring, which was convenient for travelers. However, due to road surface repairs, the service was suspended. Now that the road surface and bridge construction have been completed at the end of September, the provincial government has been petitioned to organize a long-distance bus management office to trial the long-distance bus service. The route starts from Zhongshan in Zhenjiang, passing through Paifang, Qiaojiamen, Xia Xin Dian, Weigang, Dongchang Street, Luoyangguan, Xia Dian, and ends at the East Gate of Jurong, for a total of nine stops and a total length of 43 kilometers. The fare is 3 cents per kilometer (equivalent to 1.8 li). The fare from Zhenjiang to Jurong is 1.29 yuan. It is scheduled to officially open on the 12th of this month. Buses will depart from Zhenjiang and Jurong every day at 8:00 a.m., 10:30 a.m., 1:00 p.m., and 3:30 p.m.

Implementation of Military-Industrial Policy for Huai River Project 107

The Huai River project started in mid-April. At that time, because the Liang Guanying troops stationed in Jiangbei participated with two brigades of soldiers, the progress of the project was very rapid. Since the Liang troops were ordered to be transferred to Anhui in July, the labor force was lost, and the project was announced to be suspended. Although the project is now being carried out simultaneously into the Yangtze River and into the sea, the funding is still insufficient and the number of hired workers is small. The commander-in-chief of the First Route Army, Chen Diaoyuan, who is currently stationed in Jiangbei, believes that the bandit atmosphere in Jiangbei has gradually subsided, and there is no need for heavy troops to suppress it. He is also willing to allocate two brigades of soldiers to participate in the project. Chen has now reached an agreement with the Huai River Commission in Nanjing, and will continue to follow the previous method. As soon as Chen returns to Pukou from Nanjing, he will send a team to the construction area to work.

Hefei

Measures for Reorganizing the County's Security Team 112

The mission of Security Director Zhang Yawei's current inspection is to reorganize the Hefei, Lu'an, and Shouxian security groups into security teams, and to supervise the counties in the bandit areas to handle the aftermath. As for the establishment of the security team, it has been decided by the county meeting that: (1) Three squadrons and one independent platoon will be organized in the urban area, and five squadrons will be organized in the rural area; (2) The urban area expenses will be supplemented by 1.2% of the land and various agencies, and the rural area expenses will require 100,000 yuan per year, which will be supplemented by 4% of the land; (3) Clear the villages and severely punish several group leaders who collude with bandits or harbor bandits as a warning; (4) Strictly prohibit the planting of opium.

Correspondence

Report on Chen Fu's Tragic Abduction and Murder by Chen Shuren 113

My son, Fu, studied in Soviet Russia, graduated from Sun Yat-sen University, and served as a translator in a Russian military academy for many years. Three years ago, he returned to China and traveled to Hong Kong, Shanghai, and Tianjin. He was once arrested in Tianjin on suspicion of being a communist, but was released without incident. After returning home from Tianjin last July, he dispelled all thoughts, closed his doors to study, and cut off contact with the outside world. He did not ask about anything external. In his daily life, in addition to spending most of his time in his study, he also hired a teacher to learn German. In his spare time, he grew flowers and fruits, or went horseback riding or to the movies with two or three relatives and friends. Recently, he also asked his younger brother in Shanghai to purchase a large number of ancient Chinese literature books for him to study. Unexpectedly, he went out after lunch on August 10th and never returned. Upon receiving the family report, Shuren telegraphed Chen Jitang on the 15th to investigate. Chen replied on the 17th, firmly stating that the Guangzhou authorities had not detained his son Zhiwen (Fu's other name) (the full text of the original telegram is recorded below). He then replied three more times (the full text of the original letters is recorded below) and also sent another telegram, all firmly denying the detention, only saying that he was missing. He thought that the matter was extremely secret and that there would never be a day of discovery. However, if the matter were not too tragic, and if those who heard about it did not hold extremely indignant and unfair feelings, they would not dare to risk secretly reporting it (The Guangzhou authorities mainly kept the matter extremely secret. Any slight oversight, or anyone who talked about it, would be detained and severely punished). Now, a summary of the confirmed information from various reports is as follows:

The Hong Kong conspiracy group, i.e., a certain faction who previously masterminded the assassination of Mr. Liao Zhongkai, has often fabricated baseless accusations against Shuren for the past half year due to differences in opinions and divergent paths. Even when Shuren held personal painting exhibitions in Beijing and Shanghai, he was constantly scolded by them. Shuren simply laughed it off. However, in early August, they believed that there was an opportunity to take advantage of certain matters, and made a destructive plan (this plan involves too much and will not be announced for the time being). They did not hesitate to sacrifice Shuren's son, Chen Fu. Otherwise, if Chen Fu were truly guilty, the authorities could openly arrest him or announce his crimes and execute him. Why would they perform this political "government kidnapping" that has never been heard of in history? This is too dark a secret. First, after the conspiracy group and the Guangzhou authorities reached an agreement, they gave a large sum of money and secretly sent Chen Xingou and Fei Hong, two detectives from the Guangzhou Public Security Bureau stationed in Hong Kong, back to Guangzhou. Huang Gangzhong, the secretary of the Public Security Bureau, gave them a warrant. They ambushed near the Qiaoyuan in Dongshan. When they saw Chen Fu leaving, they got on the public bus. The detectives followed him. When Fu got off at the Cangbian Road intersection, the detectives followed him and immediately arrested him and took him to the bureau. The special investigation chief, Liang Yuguang, secretly interrogated him. That night (August 10, 11 p.m.), without saying a word, they secretly transported this pure and unyielding young man, who was only 25 years old, to Nan Shi Tou and tragically shot him. They then claimed that Chen Fu was missing in order to eliminate the traces. In short, this tragic case was carried out by narrow-minded and ruthless people in order to achieve their political destructive conspiracy. They did not hesitate to use the hands of a dignified government official, using a political machine to execute it. Their dark and cruel methods were ten times worse than kidnappers tearing up the ticket. This is truly a political disgrace that has never been seen before in China and abroad. Even if we take a step back and say that Chen Fu must be punished, the most he could be sentenced to is detention, or sent to a reformatory. How could they indulge in torture to such an extreme? However, just from this point alone, we can infer and see through the position of the authorities on politics, law, morality, and human feelings, and the impact on the people. Alas, alas! Written by Chen Shuren on October 5, 1932.

Appendix: Three Telegrams from Chen Jitang (Chen Jitang Telegram) Shanghai to Mr. Chen Shuren: With utmost respect, I have respectfully read your telegram. After inquiring with Public Security Bureau Director He and Military Police Commander Lin, both stated that there was no detention of your son Zhiwen (Fu's other name). To what degree is it accurate he disappeared in Guangzhou, and when was it discovered? Please promptly check and telegraph back to facilitate investigation on my behalf. Respectfully, Chen Jitang, 17th) Printed. (Chen Jitang Letter 1) Mr. Shuren's blessing, Your wife has returned to Guangdong, and I respectfully received your letter. One thing is that your son Zhiwen has not been arrested by the Guangzhou authorities. After previously receiving your esteemed telegram, I have already replied by telegram. I trust that you are aware of this. However, according to the situation described by your daughter, it is suspected that he is missing. I have now formally instructed Public Security Bureau Director He to find a way to investigate, and I also ask your esteemed officials to assist in the process. This is my earnest request. I respectfully reply and wish you well. Yours sincerely, Chen Jitang, August 20. (Chen Jitang Letter 2) To Mr. Shuren: Regarding the matter of your son's disappearance, I have received repeated letters and telegrams and am extremely anxious. However, after investigation, the Public Security Bureau has not detained him. I have already reported the details to your wife. But your affairs are my affairs, and I have strictly instructed the Public Security Bureau to find a way to investigate and will never abandon it. Because Brother Xiangen is going to Beijing, I take this opportunity to report to you. Please advise. Chen Ji Zhuang, August 26. (This is a handwritten letter) Another reply from Chen Jitang on September 10, and a telegram on September 26, are of the same intention as above and are omitted.

Educational News

Important Elementary School News 114

Specific Standards for Civic Training, More Than 140 Items, Fully Discussed

Nanjing, 7th - The Ministry of Education's Elementary School Curriculum Civic Training Revision Committee continued its meeting on the 7th to discuss more than 140 specific standards for the elementary school civic training curriculum, and completely passed them. In terms of nature, about 70 items belong to the moral aspect, about 30 items belong to recreation, and about 20 items each belong to politics and economics. In terms of grade level, there are more than 60 items for lower grades, more than 40 items for middle grades, and more than 30 items for upper grades. Lower grades focus on recreation (such as developing hygiene habits), middle school grades focus on morality to establish a foundation, and upper grades focus on politics and economics. The special feature of this standard is the addition of economics, with special attention to production cooperation. The committee will continue to meet on the 8th to discuss the key points of training, specific standards, and organize classification.

Results of the National Central University College of Agriculture Announced 115

Nanjing, 7th - The screening examination for students of the National Central University College of Agriculture has been completed, and 143 people, including Peng Jisheng, have passed.

Jiangsu Department of Education Bans Private Middle Schools in the Provincial Capital 116

The Jiangsu Department of Education recently secretly investigated the management of private middle schools in Zhenjiang. According to the investigation, the foundation of the private Jingjiang Junior Vocational Middle School is very simple, the content is corrupt, and the accumulated expenses exceed 5,000 yuan, making it difficult to maintain. The private Jiangsu Junior Vocational Middle School has exhausted its funds, is poorly managed, and reports untruthfully, intending to deceive. The private Zhenjiang Junior Vocational Middle School, under the name of a vocational school, still runs ordinary courses, and also enrolls second-year students when it is opened, all of which violate the rules. The private Southeast Junior Vocational Middle School did not apply for establishment and the board of directors enrolled students without authorization. The ordinary courses enrolled deviate from the purpose of vocational education. The normal school is not suitable for private schools to run. Also, at the beginning of its operation, all grades recruited second-year students, which is inconsistent with current laws and regulations. Director Zhou believes that these schools are poorly managed and should be strictly banned to avoid misleading young people. He ordered that Jingjiang Vocational Middle School be disbanded immediately and be responsible for the ending by the school, the Jiangsu Vocational Middle School's board of directors be revoked, and the original application for establishment not be approved. Zhenjiang Vocational Middle School should change its ordinary courses to business courses according to the approved original plan. The existing third grade should extend the term to complete training. Southeast Vocational Middle School should abolish the ordinary and normal courses and change to business or other vocational courses. The enrolled second-year students should be uniformly changed to first-year students to comply with the Ministry of Education's orders, and follow the prescribed registration procedures and apply for approval in accordance with the law.

Over the Past Twenty Years 117

Statistics of Elementary School Teachers in Jiangsu Province: The United Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu has compiled statistics on the number of elementary school teachers in various counties of Jiangsu Province from the first year to the twentieth year of the Republic of China, comparing them year by year and making a general comparison every five years. Here are some of the main points:

(1) The total number of teachers in the counties increased from 9,312 in the first year to 19,332 in the twentieth year, an increase of 10,020, or more than 2.2 times, with an average annual increase of 527 teachers (according to the statistics, from the first year to the twentieth year, the number of schools increased by 1.77 times, the number of classes increased by 2.2 times, the number of children increased by 3.2 times, and the funding increased by 3.23 times).

(2) Comparing the number of teachers increased in each year with the previous year, the order of the amount is as follows: First, the 17th year, 2,300 people; Second, the 4th year, 1,122 people; Third, the 0th year, 974 people; Fourth, the 1st year, 961 people; Fifth, the 3rd year, 933 people; Sixth, the 14th year, 839 people; Seventh, the 6th year, 765 people; Eighth, the 5th year, 740 people; Ninth, the 8th year, 727 people; Tenth, the 7th year, 691 people; Eleventh, the 2nd year, 680 people; Twelfth, the 9th year, 670 people; Thirteenth, the 12th year, 524 people; Fourteenth, the 20th year, 312 people; Fifteenth, the 18th year, 236 people; Sixteenth, the 6th year, 226 people; Seventeenth, the 13th year, a decrease of 171 people; Eighteenth, the 19th year, a decrease of 617 people; Nineteenth, the 15th year, a decrease of 2,234 people.

(3) Observing the above statistics, it can be seen that the number of schools increased in each year did not increase annually, and the increase and decrease were quite inconsistent. The increase was the largest in the 17th year and the smallest in the 13th year. Especially in the 15th and 19th years, there were reductions compared to the previous year, totaling 2,851 people.

(4) Making a comparison every five years, the 5th year increased by 3,475 people compared to the 1st year, the 10th year increased by 3,288 people compared to the 5th year, the 15th year increased by 261 people compared to the 10th year, and the 20th year increased by 2 and 96 people compared to the 15th year. On average, each five-year period increased by 868 people, the second five-year period increased by 657 people, the third five-year period increased by only 52 people, and the fourth five-year period increased by 599 people. It can be seen that the number of teachers increased more in the early Republic of China, and the reduction in the middle was special.

(5) Comparing the situation of each county, the most in the first year was 774 in Wujin, and the least was 4 in Yangzhou. In the twentieth year, the most was 1,436 in Wuxi, and the least was 32 in Yangzhou.

(6) In the 20 years, the number of teachers in each county has increased and decreased from time to time. Comparing the 10th year with the 1st year, the counties with a decrease are Wujiang and Dangshan. Comparing the 20th year with the 1st year, the counties with a decrease are Shanghai, Taicang, and Shiying.

(7) In the first year, there were 32 counties with less than 100 teachers, including Xuhai and Ningyang. In the twentieth year, there were only 10 counties with less than 100 teachers, including Yangzhou, Baoying, Siyang, Jiangpu, Donghai, Pi, Gan Yu, Yizheng, Gaoyou, and Jiangning.

(8) The proportion of teachers increased in each county varies greatly. For example, comparing the 20th year with the 1st year, the largest increase was in Lishui, from 6 to 107 people, an increase of 18 times. The smallest increase was in Pi County, from 53 to 81 people, less than half. The remaining counties with an increase of more than 2 times include Jurong, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Liuhe, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Yangzhou, Chuansha, Shishan, Haimen, Jingjiang, Nantong, Rugao, Taixing, Lianshui, Funing, Yancheng, Xinghua, Taixian, Tongshan, Fengxian, Pei County, Yangshan, Suqian, Donghai, Guanyun, Ganyu, Suining, and Shuyang, a total of 21 counties.

Local News

Circular from the Municipal Education Bureau 118

No Celebrations to be Held this Year on National Day: The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued a circular yesterday to its affiliated schools and agencies, stating, "It is hereby notified that Circular No. 8085 from the Ministry of Education states: 'It is hereby notified that Circular No. 3896 from the Executive Yuan states: "It is hereby approved the official letter from the Central Secretariat stating: "It is found that the Central Government has decided on this year's National Day commemoration. During this national crisis, only commemorations will be held regarding the ceremony, and no celebrations will be held. All agencies will not be closed on this day, and will continue to work as usual." In addition to dispatching telegrams to the party departments of each province for compliance, this is specifically communicated for your information. Please promptly forward to all affiliated agencies for their information, etc.' In light of this approval, in addition to the issuance of orders, it is hereby ordered that the Bureau be informed and that the affiliated agencies be informed.' Accordingly, the educational agencies should continue to work as usual, and the schools should continue to hold classes as usual. In addition to the issuance of orders, it is hereby ordered that the Bureau be informed of this order. This order is issued on October 7th, the 21st year of the Republic of China, by Director Pan Gongzhan."

Chinese Youth Handball Competition 140

Sun Daosheng Overcomes Hong Yukui. The Old General's Might Still Exists, and a Second-Place Finish is Promising.

Both Battles End 21-19.

In this year's Youth Association handball competition, Sun Daosheng is the only surviving veteran who has been consistently outstanding for more than ten years. Yesterday, he met Hong Yukui, the defending champion, whom the audience considered to be the only promising young hero in the future. Between the old and the young, there were all kinds of tricks and wonderful performances. At the beginning of the first game, Hong saved the ball several times, escaping from death, creating a superior situation and rising steadily, from 14-4 to 19-12. At that time, Sun was at a disadvantage, but as soon as the opportunity came, he immediately reversed the situation and won with 21-19. The situation in the second game was tighter than before, and both sides seemed to be at a horizontal level, with the difference always between one or two points. As a result, Sun won again with 21-19, and a second-place finish is very promising. Although Hong lost, his brave spirit and superb skills were still appreciated by the audience. A hero lost to a good man is also reasonable. Zhu Shi defeated Ma Ling 2-0 (Luan). Jing Fan Hua defeated Zhong Zhong (Dong) 2-0. The battle between Hong Rulin and Lu Luosheng was also very close. Lu took the lead and won the first game with 21-16. Unexpectedly, Hong worked hard to counterattack and won the last victory by winning two consecutive games with 21-6 and 21-11.

Local News

Song Ziwen Flew to Shanghai Yesterday 146

Seeking Wang's Opinion on the Report

Scheduled to Return to Beijing Today to Continue Discussions

Song Ziwen, the Acting President of the Executive Yuan, accompanied by Chu Minyi, the Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and others, flew from Beijing to Shanghai yesterday afternoon. According to Song, he came to Shanghai to seek Mr. Wang Jingwei's opinion on the League of Nations Investigation Team's report and will return to Beijing within days to continue the discussion of the Foreign Affairs Committee. Details are recorded below.

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 147

Song attended the Foreign Affairs Committee the day before yesterday afternoon to discuss in detail the contents of the Investigation Team's report. After compiling the opinions of the various committees, Song took them with him yesterday morning at about 11:00 AM and flew to Shanghai on the Sikorsky aircraft, arriving at Hongqiao Airport at 12:25 PM. After getting off the plane, Song took his own car and returned to his residence at 12:45 PM to rest. Those who came with Song were Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, Shen Yiqing, Counselor of the Ministry of Finance, Huang Chun, staff member, and Guan Engineer. After arriving at his residence, Song also invited Chu Minyi and others to lunch at his home. Chu did not leave until about 2:00 PM.

Song's Statement 148

After returning to his residence, according to his statement to the reporters, the League of Nations Investigation Team's report is being carefully studied by the various central committees and the Foreign Affairs Committee. Before the central government's opinion is determined, he personally is not able to express his opinion. He came to Shanghai today specifically to meet with Mr. Wang Jingwei to seek Wang's opinion on the report. After meeting with Wang, he will return to Beijing to continue the discussion.

Visiting Wang This Morning 149

After Song arrived in Shanghai, he had not yet met with Wang as of last night. This is because Wang was following doctor's orders and could not receive guests to avoid fatigue. However, Mr. Chu Minyi took the report and his opinions to Noir Hospital at 5:00 PM last night to report to Wang. It lasted about half an hour, and at 5:45 PM he returned to Wang's residence on Rue Bourgeois. It is reported that Song is scheduled to visit Wang at the hospital this morning and will return to Beijing by the original plane this afternoon.

Xu Shiying chaired the meeting, reporting on the disaster situation in the Northeast and the association's work progress. In addition to the disaster situation in Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Harbin, which was recorded in yesterday's newspaper, details are recorded below.

Chairman's Report 151

During the meeting, Mr. Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Association, stood up and reported, "I am grateful for your presence at our association today. I and my colleagues in this association follow the lead of various social groups and philanthropists, and do our best to provide relief and assistance to those in need. We have been doing this for years. In peacetime, we provide relief to those affected by floods, droughts, and other disasters, and rescue the dying and help the injured. My colleagues are already extremely saddened by these events. This time, in providing relief to the disaster in the Northeast, I feel particularly sad. In terms of our duty, we cannot refuse. In terms of humanity, we must act immediately. Now, I will briefly report on the establishment process and resolutions of this association, as well as the situation of the emergency relief work being carried out in the most severely affected disaster areas in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces. Please provide guidance. This association was formed by the most historical and successful charity organizations in Shanghai, and its purpose is purely charitable and its procedures are righteous. It was established on August 23rd of this year at the Renji Hall on Yunnan Road in this city. There are a total of nine united charity groups, named as follows: Chinese Red Cross Society, China International Famine Relief Commission, World Red Swastika Society, Chinese Jisheng Society, Lianyi Charity Society, Huisheng Charity Society, Chinese Moral Improvement Society, Pushan Villa, Xinwei Relief Society. The severity of the floods in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces this year is unprecedented. The brief situation of the investigation report of this association is not even a fraction of the whole picture. I have specially printed and distributed copies so that you can get a glimpse. Mr. Yang Zigong, the relief representative of the four northeastern provinces, recently came to Shanghai from Beiping to report to the meeting. He said that representatives of the disaster victims in various places have come to Beiping to beg for help, and the number is endless. It is early winter in the borderlands, and the weather is already very cold. Currently, the relief supplies needed most are grain, as well as leather and cotton clothing. The association is now planning to quickly raise large sums of relief money and purchase relief supplies to carry out emergency relief. In addition to the 150,000 yuan that the association and its united charity groups have advanced, the Relief Committee has allocated 50,000 yuan, and the Penang Reading Newspaper Society has donated 30,000 yuan. It is planned to purchase winter clothing in Harbin and distribute it selectively. We will also actively solicit donations in various ways to continue to provide relief, food, or cash. There is no need to worry about the distribution of relief supplies by this association, because the united charity groups, such as the Chinese Red Cross Society and the World Red Cross Society, have been providing relief in the three northeastern provinces for many years and have many branches that can distribute supplies on the spot, accurately to each household and name. The income and expenditure of relief funds will be strictly in accordance with the rules, and every penny will go to the disaster-stricken compatriots. However, the water damage in Jilin and Heilongjiang is severe, the number of disaster victims is large, and the disaster area is extremely vast. It is necessary to rely on the charitable men and women from China and abroad, to work together and cooperate to rescue the disaster and reverse the catastrophe. You are enthusiastic about good deeds and act bravely when you see what is right. Whenever a disaster comes, you shout loudly and call on the government and society to work together to provide relief. Now, I respectfully ask for the sympathy of human mutual assistance, the merit of rescuing the drowning and helping the hungry, and to vigorously publicize and solicit donations on our behalf. Then, to get the northeastern disaster victims out of the water and fire, and to put them to rest on their beds, depends on the benevolence of the benevolent. I and others respectfully represent the 30 million disaster victims in the Northeast and thank you very much.

Responses from Hosts and Guests 152

After the chairman's speech, Zheng Hongnian, Qu Yingguang, and Wang Xiaolai successively gave speeches, stating the importance of rescuing the refugees in the Northeast is no less important than assisting the volunteer army. Qu also used the analogy of a daughter being taken away, and if the mother's family ignores it, after a long time, the daughter will have no good feelings for the mother's family and will instead harbor resentment. He cited the example of Germany's defeat in the European War because its people ran out of food. Wang used the analogy of treating illnesses with both offensive and palliative prescriptions, which were extremely alarming. Later, Qian Hua, representing the reporters, gave a reply, stating the three major significance of rescuing the refugees in the Northeast in terms of international anti-Japanese and anti-puppet, and took the essence of people's cooperation as the foundation for recovering the lost land in the Northeast.

Qu and Others Going North 153

The association's executive directors decided in a previous meeting to send the executive director Qu Yingguang, Wang Peiyuan of the Red Cross Society, and Feng Yangshan of the Chinese Jisheng Society north to distribute relief. Therefore, Qu said during yesterday's meeting that he would go north within two weeks, if there were no special reasons, to discuss relief methods with Mr. Xiong Bingsan of the Tianjin Office. In any case, he would ensure that the relief funds and materials were transported to the disaster area so that the refugees could benefit from them and the money would not be wasted.

Donation Situation 154

Since the association was established, few donation brochures have been distributed, so it has received only more than 6,000 yuan in donations. In addition, the nine initiating groups have advanced 150,000 yuan, the Relief Committee has allocated 50,000 yuan, and the Penang Reading Newspaper Society has donated 30,000 yuan. (This total amount of 60,000 yuan has not been used for a long time because the receiving agency was unclear. Recently, 30,000 yuan was allocated to the Northeast Relief Association and distributed by General Zhu Ziqiao, and 30,000 yuan was allocated to the United Relief Association.) Recently, it has been slightly obtained. A certain number of large companies in this city have agreed to donate 5% of their sales proceeds within four days, and it is scheduled for the 16th and 26th of this month, when the Wanguo Jiangwan Yinxiang Sanhui will volunteer to race horses at Jiangwan, and the proceeds from the sale of tickets will be used for relief.

Raising Emergency Relief 155

The association believes that the refugees in the Northeast have suffered both war and floods, and the weather is getting colder, so relief is more urgent than ever. It has repeatedly published articles in newspapers to appeal to the public. The association has now received a report on the flooding in Jilin and Heilongjiang. More than 40,000 refugees in Yilan County, Jilin Province, are lacking food. 7,500 households in Weihe County have flooded houses. The total losses are about 3 million. In the deepest part of Harbin, the water is 14 or 15 feet deep. The Red Cross Society has successively provided relief and accommodated 23,267 refugees. About 80,000 refugees who have escaped to high ground refuse to give up their goods and still live in buildings. About 100,000 people are still living in buildings. The flood-affected area in Heilongjiang Province is even wider. Longjiang, Qinggang, Yalu, Nehe, Gannan, Hulan, Tonghe, and Mulan counties have all become swamps. The loss of life and property is countless. The refugees are hungry and cold. Various charity groups and the Northeast Refugee Relief Association invite the press to take photographs.

They are exposed to the elements and are in a terrible state. It was decided to first carry out emergency relief in the most severely affected disaster areas in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces. It is hoped that compatriots across the country will follow the principle of saving the people is saving the country, and generously donate money to contribute to this good cause.

Mrs. Moore of the United States Arrives in Shanghai 156

Representing German People

Comforting the 19th Route Army

Mrs. Moore, a German-American residing in Germany, representing various sectors of the German public, came to Shanghai to comfort our anti-Japanese 19th Route Army. She arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 6:00 a.m. aboard the "Africa," the first Far East-bound mail ship of the Danish East Asiatic Company. After arriving, Mrs. Moore stayed at the Astor House Hotel on the Bund and immediately sent telegrams to various newspaper reporters, inviting them for a conversation.

This Mission 157

Mrs. Moore first described her mission for this trip, stating, "I am here purely to represent various sectors of the German public and to comfort the soldiers of your country's 19th Route Army who bravely resisted the aggressors. The entire German people express their deepest sympathy for your country and your country's loyal and brave 19th Route Army. When the 19th Army was resisting Japan in Shanghai, the entire German people were extremely concerned. After your country's English version of the 'National Forum' was sent to Germany, we were extremely pleased with the detailed accounts of the 19th Army and the portraits of its soldiers. We were also amazed that the 19th Army was resisting Japan with such meager strength. Therefore, people from all walks of life in Germany, as well as major corporations, are willing to contribute to comfort the soldiers of the 19th Army. Since I had a trip to your country, they entrusted me with the task of delivering these gifts. However, the German side was not sure what items would be most useful, so they could not rashly send them. Therefore, I only brought various samples this time, waiting for the authorities of the 19th Route Army to decide what is needed and in what quantity, and then I will send a telegram to the relevant German companies to arrange for shipment to your country. Currently, the value of the gifts prepared by the German side to comfort the 19th Army is at least 5,000 US dollars."

European and American Attitudes Toward China 158

Mrs. Moore then spoke about the attitudes of European and American countries toward China, saying, "After leaving Germany, I went to various European and American countries for observation. Except for Soviet Russia, I have visited almost all major European and American countries. Some people in Europe and America do have sympathy for China, but most of them do not have an accurate understanding of China due to a lack of knowledge of the situation. When I was in Geneva, the news I heard about China was mostly malicious propaganda deliberately spread by a certain party. This should also be remedied in international public opinion. I believe that since the Chinese side now has a very large radio station, it should report to Geneva as soon as possible and transmit all the latest news, shifting the world's attention. Because propaganda is extremely important in the international arena now." She also said, "If the Chinese government could provide a nominally Chinese public opinion circle with considerable assistance, she would be very willing to take responsibility for external propaganda on behalf of China."

Lytton Report 159

Yesterday, Mrs. Moore also criticized the League of Nations investigation team's Lytton Report, saying, "That report is truly a boastful work. I had already heard about its contents when I was in Europe. People in Europe and America are very dissatisfied with the report, saying that it is not only powerless but also fails to distinguish right from wrong. However, the international community expresses unanimous admiration for China's diplomatic talents. The Chinese embassy in Germany is able to integrate well with the entire German public. She is also friendly with people such as Liang Long, the embassy counselor. Mr. Liang even asked her to convey his regards to friends in Shanghai during this trip to Shanghai. European and American countries not only admire China's diplomatic talents, but also unanimously praise Dr. Wellington Koo's recent work as being extremely valuable." While saying this, Mrs. Moore also said, "You can deeply believe my words. I can even cite an example to show the respect and love of European and American people for your country's diplomats. Several months ago, in the Mediterranean, when the French mail ship 'Georges Philippar' had an accident, the bad news came that Minister Shih Chao-chi, who was negotiating at the League of Nations, had also died in the disaster. All sectors in Europe and America were greatly shocked and even flew flags at half-mast to express their condolences. Then they learned that the facts were wrong, and they burst into laughter."

Talking About General Ma 160

Mrs. Moore then took out the English version of General Ma Zhanshan's anti-Japanese telegram and told reporters that European and American people not only admired your country's 19th Route Army, but also greatly admired General Ma Zhanshan. If General Ma Zhanshan wanted to raise funds in Europe and America at this time, I can guarantee that tens of millions could be raised in 48 hours, because all parties in Europe and America unanimously admire General Ma Zhanshan's character.

Going to the Capital 161

Mrs. Moore then said that she would be going to the capital in the near future, but the date has not been determined. She has many missions for this trip, but other than comforting the 19th Route Army soldiers, she cannot announce anything else. She gained a good understanding of the situation in various countries towards China during her trip to Europe and America, so she intends to meet with the Chinese government authorities. Finally, she led the reporters to see the consolation samples she brought, which totaled more than a hundred kinds, mostly medical supplies for wounded soldiers' hospitals. There were also dozens of kinds of cigarettes, but they were all samples.

The Water Company Will Change Water Rates 164

Notification to All Users Yesterday

Since the British-owned Shanghai Water Company changed to a meter system, water rates have increased sharply, in some cases by as much as nine times. Various rental agencies and public groups have negotiated with the company directly and indirectly. The company also felt that the increase was too large and issued a notice yesterday, notifying all users, "Regarding the bills you sent, which are calculated based on the water meter reading, if they exceed the amount paid under the previous monthly system by too much, please notify our company so that we can investigate the cause of the excess use. In order to temporarily change the water rate during the investigation period, please include the account number of the location in all the notification letters you drop off for reference. We hereby notify you."

The Shanghai South Bus Workers' Strike Was Resolved Yesterday With the Signing of an Agreement 165

The Company Will Pay One Month's Salary

All Workers Will Be Reinstated When Business Resumes

Although the Shanghai South Bus Company's strike dispute has been mediated by party and government agencies many times, it has been impossible to resolve it due to the insistence of both labor and management. The Bureau of Social Affairs convened a final mediation meeting again yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m. Representatives from the labor side Qian Shunlv and Hu Jinshan, representatives from the management side Xu Jiqin, and Yu Zhongbiao from the Municipal Party Department attended. Peng Zhenqiu from the Bureau of Social Affairs chaired the meeting, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. After a long period of separate discussions, an agreement was finally signed at 7:00 p.m. The original text of the agreement is recorded below: (1) The company will lend each worker one month's salary. If the business cannot be resumed in the future, it will be used as severance pay. (2) When the company resumes business, all original workers will be reinstated. The loaned salary will be deducted in installments from the monthly salary, but if the company reduces its scope and cannot hire all of them, it may hire from the original workers, but may not hire new workers. (3) 20% of the salary for April and 10% of the salary for May (calculated according to the original salary ratio, those who have received enough are not included in this example). (4) The arrears of salary and the loaned one month's salary shall be paid first from the company's property. (5) The money owed by the workers to the company in the past will be allowed to be deducted. (6) When the company pays the above salary, the workers should return the copper license plate clothing, and at the same time the company must return the insurance policies of each worker (the price and the company's accounts are not cleared are not included in this example). (7) When the salary is paid, the workers shall all withdraw from the company.
